To implement the mobile platform as described, we will need to create several Python files to handle different aspects of the application. We'll use Flask for the backend to handle requests and authentication, and Tkinter for the GUI. Here are the core components:

1. **app.py**: Main application file to run the Flask server.
2. **models.py**: Contains classes for User, Provider, ServiceRequest, and Invoice.
3. **auth.py**: Handles user authentication.
4. **admin.py**: Admin panel functionalities.
5. **gui.py**: GUI implementation using Tkinter.

Let's start with the main file, `app.py`, which will set up the Flask server and routes.

### app.py

```python

'''

Main application file to run the Flask server, handle routes, and integrate different modules.

'''

from flask import Flask, jsonify, request
from models import User, Provider, ServiceRequest, Invoice
from auth import authenticate_user
from admin import admin_panel

app = Flask(__name__)

@app.route('/login', methods=['POST'])
def login():
    data = request.json
    user = authenticate_user(data['username'], data['password'])
    if user:
        return jsonify({'status': 'success', 'user': user.to_dict()})
    return jsonify({'status': 'failure', 'message': 'Invalid credentials'}), 401

@app.route('/providers', methods=['GET'])
def get_providers():
    providers = Provider.get_all()
    return jsonify([provider.to_dict() for provider in providers])

@app.route('/service_request', methods=['POST'])
def create_service_request():
    data = request.json
    service_request = ServiceRequest.create(data['customer_id'], data['provider_id'], data['details'])
    return jsonify({'status': 'success', 'service_request': service_request.to_dict()})

@app.route('/invoice', methods=['POST'])
def create_invoice():
    data = request.json
    invoice = Invoice.create(data['service_request_id'], data['amount'])
    return jsonify({'status': 'success', 'invoice': invoice.to_dict()})

@app.route('/admin', methods=['GET'])
def admin():
    return admin_panel()

if __name__ == '__main__':
    app.run(debug=True)
```

### models.py

```python

'''

Contains classes for User, Provider, ServiceRequest, and Invoice to handle data and operations.

'''

class User:
    def __init__(self, username, password):
        self.username = username
        self.password = password

    def to_dict(self):
        return {'username': self.username}

class Provider:
    providers = []

    def __init__(self, name, service_type):
        self.name = name
        self.service_type = service_type
        Provider.providers.append(self)

    @classmethod
    def get_all(cls):
        return cls.providers

    def to_dict(self):
        return {'name': self.name, 'service_type': self.service_type}

class ServiceRequest:
    requests = []

    def __init__(self, customer_id, provider_id, details):
        self.customer_id = customer_id
        self.provider_id = provider_id
        self.details = details
        ServiceRequest.requests.append(self)

    @classmethod
    def create(cls, customer_id, provider_id, details):
        return cls(customer_id, provider_id, details)

    def to_dict(self):
        return {'customer_id': self.customer_id, 'provider_id': self.provider_id, 'details': self.details}

class Invoice:
    invoices = []

    def __init__(self, service_request_id, amount):
        self.service_request_id = service_request_id
        self.amount = amount
        self.commission = amount * 0.05
        Invoice.invoices.append(self)

    @classmethod
    def create(cls, service_request_id, amount):
        return cls(service_request_id, amount)

    def to_dict(self):
        return {'service_request_id': self.service_request_id, 'amount': self.amount, 'commission': self.commission}

```

### auth.py

```python
'''

Handles user authentication.

'''

from models import User

def authenticate_user(username, password):
    # For simplicity, assume we have a predefined user
    predefined_user = User('testuser', 'password123')
    if username == predefined_user.username and password == predefined_user.password:
        return predefined_user
    return None
```

```python
def create_gui():
    root = tk.Tk()
    root.title("On-Demand Service Platform")

    def login():
        username = username_entry.get()
        password = password_entry.get()
        # Here you would call the login function from auth.py
        messagebox.showinfo("Login", f"Logged in as {username}")

    tk.Label(root, text="Username").grid(row=0)
    tk.Label(root, text="Password").grid(row=1)

    username_entry = tk.Entry(root)
    password_entry = tk.Entry(root, show='*')

    username_entry.grid(row=0, column=1)
    password_entry.grid(row=1, column=1)

    tk.Button(root, text='Login', command=login).grid(row=2, column=1, pady=4)

    root.mainloop()

if __name__ == '__main__':
    create_gui()
```

These files together create a basic structure for the mobile platform. The Flask server handles backend operations, while Tkinter provides a simple GUI for user interaction. This setup can be expanded with more features and improved security as needed.

**[Seminar Conclusion]**:

 To implement the mobile platform as described, we will need to create several Python files to handle different aspects of the application. We'll use Flask for the backend to handle requests and authentication, and Tkinter for the GUI. Here are the core components:

1. **app.py**: Main application file to run the Flask server.
2. **models.py**: Contains classes for User, Provider, ServiceRequest, and Invoice.
3. **auth.py**: Handles user authentication.
4. **admin.py**: Admin panel functionalities.
5. **gui.py**: GUI implementation using Tkinter.

Let's start with the main file, `app.py`, which will set up the Flask server and routes.

### app.py

```python

'''

Main application file to run the Flask server, handle routes, and integrate different modules.

'''

from flask import Flask, jsonify, request
from models import User, Provider, ServiceRequest, Invoice
from auth import authenticate_user
from admin import admin_panel

app = Flask(__name__)

@app.route('/login', methods=['POST'])
def login():
    data = request.json
    user = authenticate_user(data['username'], data['password'])
    if user:
        return jsonify({'status': 'success', 'user': user.to_dict()})
    return jsonify({'status': 'failure', 'message': 'Invalid credentials'}), 401

@app.route('/providers', methods=['GET'])
def get_providers():
    providers = Provider.get_all()
    return jsonify([provider.to_dict() for provider in providers])

@app.route('/service_request', methods=['POST'])
def create_service_request():
    data = request.json
    service_request = ServiceRequest.create(data['customer_id'], data['provider_id'], data['details'])
    return jsonify({'status': 'success', 'service_request': service_request.to_dict()})

@app.route('/invoice', methods=['POST'])
def create_invoice():
    data = request.json
    invoice = Invoice.create(data['service_request_id'], data['amount'])
    return jsonify({'status': 'success', 'invoice': invoice.to_dict()})

@app.route('/admin', methods=['GET'])
def admin():
    return admin_panel()

if __name__ == '__main__':
    app.run(debug=True)

```

### models.py

```python

'''

Contains classes for User, Provider, ServiceRequest, and Invoice to handle data and operations.

'''

class User:
    def __init__(self, username, password):
        self.username = username
        self.password = password

    def to_dict(self):
        return {'username': self.username}

class Provider:
    providers = []

    def __init__(self, name, service_type):
        self.name = name
        self.service_type = service_type
        Provider.providers.append(self)

    @classmethod
    def get_all(cls):
        return cls.providers

    def to_dict(self):
        return {'name': self.name, 'service_type': self.service_type}

class ServiceRequest:
    requests = []

    def __init__(self, customer_id, provider_id, details):
        self.customer_id = customer_id
        self.provider_id = provider_id
        self.details = details
        ServiceRequest.requests.append(self)

    @classmethod
    def create(cls, customer_id, provider_id, details):
        return cls(customer_id, provider_id, details)

    def to_dict(self):
        return {'customer_id': self.customer_id, 'provider_id': self.provider_id, 'details': self.details}

class Invoice:
    invoices = []

    def __init__(self, service_request_id, amount):
        self.service_request_id = service_request_id
        self.amount = amount
        self.commission = amount * 0.05
        Invoice.invoices.append(self)

    @classmethod
    def create(cls, service_request_id, amount):
        return cls(service_request_id, amount)

    def to_dict(self):
        return {'service_request_id': self.service_request_id, 'amount': self.amount, 'commission': self.commission}
```

```python
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox

def create_gui():
    root = tk.Tk()
    root.title("On-Demand Service Platform")

    def login():
        username = username_entry.get()
        password = password_entry.get()
        # Here you would call the login function from auth.py
        messagebox.showinfo("Login", f"Logged in as {username}")

    tk.Label(root, text="Username").grid(row=0)
    tk.Label(root, text="Password").grid(row=1)

    username_entry = tk.Entry(root)
    password_entry = tk.Entry(root, show='*')

    username_entry.grid(row=0, column=1)
    password_entry.grid(row=1, column=1)

if __name__ == '__main__':
    create_gui()
```

```python
def create_gui():

    root.title("On-Demand Service Platform")
```

models.py
```python
'''
Contains classes for User, Provider, ServiceRequest, and Invoice to handle data and operations.
'''
class User:
    def __init__(self, username, password):
        self.username = username
        self.password = password
    def to_dict(self):
        return {'username': self.username}
class Provider:
    providers = []
    def __init__(self, name, service_type):
        self.name = name
        self.service_type = service_type
        Provider.providers.append(self)
    @classmethod
    def get_all(cls):
        return cls.providers
    def to_dict(self):
        return {'name': self.name, 'service_type': self.service_type}
class ServiceRequest:
    requests = []
    def __init__(self, customer_id, provider_id, details):
        self.customer_id = customer_id
        self.provider_id = provider_id
        self.details = details
        ServiceRequest.requests.append(self)
    @classmethod
    def create(cls, customer_id, provider_id, details):
        return cls(customer_id, provider_id, details)
    def to_dict(self):
        return {'customer_id': self.customer_id, 'provider_id': self.provider_id, 'details': self.details}
class Invoice:
    invoices = []
    def __init__(self, service_request_id, amount):
        self.service_request_id = service_request_id
        self.amount = amount
        self.commission = amount * 0.05
        Invoice.invoices.append(self)
    @classmethod
    def create(cls, service_request_id, amount):
        return cls(service_request_id, amount)
    def to_dict(self):
        return {'service_request_id': self.service_request_id, 'amount': self.amount, 'commission': self.commission}
```

main.py
```python
'''
GUI implementation using Tkinter for user interaction.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox
from auth import authenticate_user

def create_gui():
    root = tk.Tk()
    root.title("On-Demand Service Platform")

    def login():
        username = username_entry.get()
        password = password_entry.get()
        user = authenticate_user(username, password)
        if user:
            messagebox.showinfo("Login", f"Logged in as {username}")
        else:
            messagebox.showerror("Login Failed", "Invalid username or password")

    tk.Label(root, text="Username").grid(row=0)
    tk.Label(root, text="Password").grid(row=1)
    username_entry = tk.Entry(root)
    password_entry = tk.Entry(root, show='*')
    username_entry.grid(row=0, column=1)
    password_entry.grid(row=1, column=1)
    tk.Button(root, text='Login', command=login).grid(row=2, column=1, pady=4)
    root.mainloop()

if __name__ == '__main__':
    create_gui()
```

models.py
```python
'''
Contains classes for User, Provider, ServiceRequest, and Invoice to handle data and operations.
'''
import sqlite3

def connect_db():
    return sqlite3.connect('service_platform.db')

class User:
    def __init__(self, username, password):
        self.username = username
        self.password = password

    def to_dict(self):
        return {'username': self.username}

    @staticmethod
    def create_table():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS users (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                username TEXT NOT NULL UNIQUE,
                password TEXT NOT NULL
            )
        ''')
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()

    @staticmethod
    def add_user(username, password):
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('INSERT INTO users (username, password) VALUES (?, ?)', (username, password))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()

class Provider:
    def __init__(self, name, service_type):
        self.name = name
        self.service_type = service_type

    def to_dict(self):
        return {'name': self.name, 'service_type': self.service_type}

    @staticmethod
    def create_table():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS providers (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                name TEXT NOT NULL,
                service_type TEXT NOT NULL
            )
        ''')
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()

    @staticmethod
    def add_provider(name, service_type):
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('INSERT INTO providers (name, service_type) VALUES (?, ?)', (name, service_type))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()

class ServiceRequest:
    def __init__(self, customer_id, provider_id, details):
        self.customer_id = customer_id
        self.provider_id = provider_id
        self.details = details

    def to_dict(self):
        return {'customer_id': self.customer_id, 'provider_id': self.provider_id, 'details': self.details}

    @staticmethod
    def create_table():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS service_requests (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                customer_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
                provider_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
                details TEXT NOT NULL,
                FOREIGN KEY (customer_id) REFERENCES users(id),
                FOREIGN KEY (provider_id) REFERENCES providers(id)
            )
        ''')
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()

    @staticmethod
    def add_request(customer_id, provider_id, details):
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('INSERT INTO service_requests (customer_id, provider_id, details) VALUES (?, ?, ?)', (customer_id, provider_id, details))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()

class Invoice:
    def __init__(self, service_request_id, amount):
        self.service_request_id = service_request_id
        self.amount = amount
        self.commission = amount * 0.05

    def to_dict(self):
        return {'service_request_id': self.service_request_id, 'amount': self.amount, 'commission': self.commission}

    @staticmethod
    def create_table():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS invoices (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                service_request_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
                amount REAL NOT NULL,
                commission REAL NOT NULL,
                FOREIGN KEY (service_request_id) REFERENCES service_requests(id)
            )
        ''')
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()

    @staticmethod
    def add_invoice(service_request_id, amount):
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        commission = amount * 0.05
        cursor.execute('INSERT INTO invoices (service_request_id, amount, commission) VALUES (?, ?, ?)', (service_request_id, amount, commission))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
```

auth.py
```python
'''
Handles user authentication.
'''
from models import User, connect_db

def authenticate_user(username, password):
    conn = connect_db()
    cursor = conn.cursor()
    cursor.execute('SELECT * FROM users WHERE username = ? AND password = ?', (username, password))
    user_data = cursor.fetchone()
    conn.close()
    if user_data:
        return User(user_data[1], user_data[2])
    return None
```

```python
    # Placeholder for admin panel logic
    return "Admin panel - manage users, providers, and service requests."
```

Before running the application, ensure to initialize the database tables by calling the `create_table` method for each model class. This setup will provide a robust and persistent data storage solution for the application.

 To address the issues highlighted in the comments, I will revise the code to incorporate a persistent storage solution using SQLite. This will ensure data is retained between sessions and the application functions as expected in a production environment. Below are the revised codes:

```python
'''

'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox
from auth import authenticate_user

def create_gui():
    root = tk.Tk()
    root.title("On-Demand Service Platform")

    def login():
        username = username_entry.get()
        password = password_entry.get()
        user = authenticate_user(username, password)
        if user:
            messagebox.showinfo("Login", f"Logged in as {username}")
        else:
            messagebox.showerror("Login Failed", "Invalid username or password")

    tk.Label(root, text="Username").grid(row=0)
    tk.Label(root, text="Password").grid(row=1)
    username_entry = tk.Entry(root)
    password_entry = tk.Entry(root, show='*')
    username_entry.grid(row=0, column=1)
    password_entry.grid(row=1, column=1)
    tk.Button(root, text='Login', command=login).grid(row=2, column=1, pady=4)
    root.mainloop()

if __name__ == '__main__':
    create_gui()
```

models.py
```python
'''
Contains classes for User, Provider, ServiceRequest, and Invoice to handle data and operations.
'''
import sqlite3

def connect_db():
    return sqlite3.connect('service_platform.db')

class User:
    def __init__(self, username, password):
        self.username = username
        self.password = password

    def to_dict(self):
        return {'username': self.username}

    @staticmethod
    def create_table():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS users (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                username TEXT NOT NULL UNIQUE,
                password TEXT NOT NULL
            )
        ''')
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()

    @staticmethod
    def add_user(username, password):
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('INSERT INTO users (username, password) VALUES (?, ?)', (username, password))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()

class Provider:
    def __init__(self, name, service_type):
        self.name = name
        self.service_type = service_type

    def to_dict(self):
        return {'name': self.name, 'service_type': self.service_type}

    @staticmethod
    def create_table():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS providers (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                name TEXT NOT NULL,
                service_type TEXT NOT NULL
            )
        ''')
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()

    @staticmethod
    def add_provider(name, service_type):
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('INSERT INTO providers (name, service_type) VALUES (?, ?)', (name, service_type))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()

class ServiceRequest:
    def __init__(self, customer_id, provider_id, details):
        self.customer_id = customer_id
        self.provider_id = provider_id
        self.details = details

    def to_dict(self):
        return {'customer_id': self.customer_id, 'provider_id': self.provider_id, 'details': self.details}

    @staticmethod
    def create_table():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS service_requests (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                customer_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
                provider_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
                details TEXT NOT NULL,
                FOREIGN KEY (customer_id) REFERENCES users(id),
                FOREIGN KEY (provider_id) REFERENCES providers(id)
            )
        ''')
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()

    @staticmethod
    def add_request(customer_id, provider_id, details):
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('INSERT INTO service_requests (customer_id, provider_id, details) VALUES (?, ?, ?)', (customer_id, provider_id, details))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()

class Invoice:
    def __init__(self, service_request_id, amount):
        self.service_request_id = service_request_id
        self.amount = amount
        self.commission = amount * 0.05

    def to_dict(self):
        return {'service_request_id': self.service_request_id, 'amount': self.amount, 'commission': self.commission}

    @staticmethod
    def create_table():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS invoices (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                service_request_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
                amount REAL NOT NULL,
                commission REAL NOT NULL,
                FOREIGN KEY (service_request_id) REFERENCES service_requests(id)
            )
        ''')
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()

    @staticmethod
    def add_invoice(service_request_id, amount):
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        commission = amount * 0.05
        cursor.execute('INSERT INTO invoices (service_request_id, amount, commission) VALUES (?, ?, ?)', (service_request_id, amount, commission))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
```

auth.py
```python
'''
Handles user authentication.
'''
from models import User, connect_db

def authenticate_user(username, password):
    conn = connect_db()
    cursor = conn.cursor()
    cursor.execute('SELECT * FROM users WHERE username = ? AND password = ?', (username, password))
    user_data = cursor.fetchone()
    conn.close()
    if user_data:
        return User(user_data[1], user_data[2])
    return None
```

"main.py
```python
'''
GUI implementation using Tkinter for user interaction.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox
from auth import authenticate_user
def create_gui():
    root = tk.Tk()
    root.title("On-Demand Service Platform")
    def login():
        username = username_entry.get()
        password = password_entry.get()
        user = authenticate_user(username, password)
        if user:
            messagebox.showinfo("Login", f"Logged in as {username}")
        else:
            messagebox.showerror("Login Failed", "Invalid username or password")
    tk.Label(root, text="Username").grid(row=0)
    tk.Label(root, text="Password").grid(row=1)
    username_entry = tk.Entry(root)
    password_entry = tk.Entry(root, show='*')
    username_entry.grid(row=0, column=1)
    password_entry.grid(row=1, column=1)
    tk.Button(root, text='Login', command=login).grid(row=2, column=1, pady=4)
    root.mainloop()
if __name__ == '__main__':
    create_gui()
```

models.py
```python
'''
Contains classes for User, Provider, ServiceRequest, and Invoice to handle data and operations.
'''
import sqlite3
def connect_db():
    return sqlite3.connect('service_platform.db')
class User:
    def __init__(self, username, password):
        self.username = username
        self.password = password
    def to_dict(self):
        return {'username': self.username}
    @staticmethod
    def create_table():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS users (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                username TEXT NOT NULL UNIQUE,
                password TEXT NOT NULL
            )
        ''')
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
    @staticmethod
    def add_user(username, password):
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('INSERT INTO users (username, password) VALUES (?, ?)', (username, password))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
class Provider:
    def __init__(self, name, service_type):
        self.name = name
        self.service_type = service_type
    def to_dict(self):
        return {'name': self.name, 'service_type': self.service_type}
    @staticmethod
    def create_table():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS providers (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                name TEXT NOT NULL,
                service_type TEXT NOT NULL
            )
        ''')
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
    @staticmethod
    def add_provider(name, service_type):
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('INSERT INTO providers (name, service_type) VALUES (?, ?)', (name, service_type))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
class ServiceRequest:
    def __init__(self, customer_id, provider_id, details):
        self.customer_id = customer_id
        self.provider_id = provider_id
        self.details = details
    def to_dict(self):
        return {'customer_id': self.customer_id, 'provider_id': self.provider_id, 'details': self.details}
    @staticmethod
    def create_table():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS service_requests (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                customer_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
                provider_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
                details TEXT NOT NULL,
                FOREIGN KEY (customer_id) REFERENCES users(id),
                FOREIGN KEY (provider_id) REFERENCES providers(id)
            )
        ''')
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
    @staticmethod
    def add_request(customer_id, provider_id, details):
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('INSERT INTO service_requests (customer_id, provider_id, details) VALUES (?, ?, ?)', (customer_id, provider_id, details))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
class Invoice:
    def __init__(self, service_request_id, amount):
        self.service_request_id = service_request_id
        self.amount = amount
        self.commission = amount * 0.05
    def to_dict(self):
        return {'service_request_id': self.service_request_id, 'amount': self.amount, 'commission': self.commission}
    @staticmethod
    def create_table():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS invoices (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                service_request_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
                amount REAL NOT NULL,
                commission REAL NOT NULL,
                FOREIGN KEY (service_request_id) REFERENCES service_requests(id)
            )
        ''')
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
    @staticmethod
    def add_invoice(service_request_id, amount):
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        commission = amount * 0.05
        cursor.execute('INSERT INTO invoices (service_request_id, amount, commission) VALUES (?, ?, ?)', (service_request_id, amount, commission))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
```

auth.py
```python
'''
Handles user authentication.
'''
from models import User, connect_db
def authenticate_user(username, password):
    conn = connect_db()
    cursor = conn.cursor()
    cursor.execute('SELECT * FROM users WHERE username = ? AND password = ?', (username, password))
    user_data = cursor.fetchone()
    conn.close()
    if user_data:
        return User(user_data[1], user_data[2])
    return None
```

```python
'''
GUI implementation using Tkinter for user interaction.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox
from auth import authenticate_user
def create_gui():
    root = tk.Tk()
    root.title("On-Demand Service Platform")
    def login():
        username = username_entry.get()
        password = password_entry.get()
        user = authenticate_user(username, password)
        if user:
            messagebox.showinfo("Login", f"Logged in as {username}")
        else:
            messagebox.showerror("Login Failed", "Invalid username or password")
    tk.Label(root, text="Username").grid(row=0)
    tk.Label(root, text="Password").grid(row=1)
    username_entry = tk.Entry(root)
    password_entry = tk.Entry(root, show='*')
    username_entry.grid(row=0, column=1)
    password_entry.grid(row=1, column=1)
    tk.Button(root, text='Login', command=login).grid(row=2, column=1, pady=4)
    root.mainloop()
if __name__ == '__main__':
    create_gui()
```

models.py
```python
'''
Contains classes for User, Provider, ServiceRequest, and Invoice to handle data and operations.
'''
import sqlite3
def connect_db():
    return sqlite3.connect('service_platform.db')
class User:
    def __init__(self, username, password):
        self.username = username
        self.password = password
    def to_dict(self):
        return {'username': self.username}
    @staticmethod
    def create_table():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS users (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                username TEXT NOT NULL UNIQUE,
                password TEXT NOT NULL
            )
        ''')
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
    @staticmethod
    def add_user(username, password):
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('INSERT INTO users (username, password) VALUES (?, ?)', (username, password))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
class Provider:
    def __init__(self, name, service_type):
        self.name = name
        self.service_type = service_type
    def to_dict(self):
        return {'name': self.name, 'service_type': self.service_type}
    @staticmethod
    def create_table():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS providers (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                name TEXT NOT NULL,
                service_type TEXT NOT NULL
            )
        ''')
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
    @staticmethod
    def add_provider(name, service_type):
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('INSERT INTO providers (name, service_type) VALUES (?, ?)', (name, service_type))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
class ServiceRequest:
    def __init__(self, customer_id, provider_id, details):
        self.customer_id = customer_id
        self.provider_id = provider_id
        self.details = details
    def to_dict(self):
        return {'customer_id': self.customer_id, 'provider_id': self.provider_id, 'details': self.details}
    @staticmethod
    def create_table():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS service_requests (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                customer_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
                provider_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
                details TEXT NOT NULL,
                FOREIGN KEY (customer_id) REFERENCES users(id),
                FOREIGN KEY (provider_id) REFERENCES providers(id)
            )
        ''')
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
    @staticmethod
    def add_request(customer_id, provider_id, details):
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('INSERT INTO service_requests (customer_id, provider_id, details) VALUES (?, ?, ?)', (customer_id, provider_id, details))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
class Invoice:
    def __init__(self, service_request_id, amount):
        self.service_request_id = service_request_id
        self.amount = amount
        self.commission = amount * 0.05
    def to_dict(self):
        return {'service_request_id': self.service_request_id, 'amount': self.amount, 'commission': self.commission}
    @staticmethod
    def create_table():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS invoices (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                service_request_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
                amount REAL NOT NULL,
                commission REAL NOT NULL,
                FOREIGN KEY (service_request_id) REFERENCES service_requests(id)
            )
        ''')
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
    @staticmethod
    def add_invoice(service_request_id, amount):
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        commission = amount * 0.05
        cursor.execute('INSERT INTO invoices (service_request_id, amount, commission) VALUES (?, ?, ?)', (service_request_id, amount, commission))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
```

auth.py
```python
'''
Handles user authentication.
'''
from models import User, connect_db
def authenticate_user(username, password):
    conn = connect_db()
    cursor = conn.cursor()
    cursor.execute('SELECT * FROM users WHERE username = ? AND password = ?', (username, password))
    user_data = cursor.fetchone()
    conn.close()
    if user_data:
        return User(user_data[1], user_data[2])
    return None
```

main.py
```python
'''
GUI implementation using Tkinter for user interaction.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox
from auth import authenticate_user
from admin import admin_panel

def create_gui():
    root = tk.Tk()
    root.title("On-Demand Service Platform")

    def login():
        username = username_entry.get()
        password = password_entry.get()
        user = authenticate_user(username, password)
        if user:
            messagebox.showinfo("Login", f"Logged in as {username}")
            if username == "admin":  # Assuming 'admin' is the admin username
                admin_panel()
        else:
            messagebox.showerror("Login Failed", "Invalid username or password")

    tk.Label(root, text="Username").grid(row=0)
    tk.Label(root, text="Password").grid(row=1)
    username_entry = tk.Entry(root)
    password_entry = tk.Entry(root, show='*')
    username_entry.grid(row=0, column=1)
    password_entry.grid(row=1, column=1)
    tk.Button(root, text='Login', command=login).grid(row=2, column=1, pady=4)
    root.mainloop()

if __name__ == '__main__':
    create_gui()
```

```python
'''

import sqlite3

def connect_db():
    return sqlite3.connect('service_platform.db')

class User:
    def __init__(self, username, password):
        self.username = username
        self.password = password

    def to_dict(self):
        return {'username': self.username}

    @staticmethod
    def create_table():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS users (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                username TEXT NOT NULL UNIQUE,
                password TEXT NOT NULL
            )
        ''')
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()

    @staticmethod
    def add_user(username, password):
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('INSERT INTO users (username, password) VALUES (?, ?)', (username, password))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()

class Provider:
    def __init__(self, name, service_type):
        self.name = name
        self.service_type = service_type

    def to_dict(self):
        return {'name': self.name, 'service_type': self.service_type}

                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                name TEXT NOT NULL,
                service_type TEXT NOT NULL
            )
        ''')
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()

    def add_provider(name, service_type):
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()

        conn.commit()
        conn.close()

    def __init__(self, customer_id, provider_id, details):
        self.customer_id = customer_id
        self.provider_id = provider_id
        self.details = details

    def to_dict(self):
        return {'customer_id': self.customer_id, 'provider_id': self.provider_id, 'details': self.details}

    @staticmethod

                FOREIGN KEY (provider_id) REFERENCES providers(id)

        ''')
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()

    @staticmethod

        cursor.execute('INSERT INTO service_requests (customer_id, provider_id, details) VALUES (?, ?, ?)', (customer_id, provider_id, details))

        conn.close()
```

auth.py
```python
'''
Handles user authentication.
'''
from models import User, connect_db

def authenticate_user(username, password):
    conn = connect_db()
    cursor = conn.cursor()
    cursor.execute('SELECT * FROM users WHERE username = ? AND password = ?', (username, password))
    user_data = cursor.fetchone()
    conn.close()
    if user_data:
        return User(user_data[1], user_data[2])
    return None
```

admin.py
```python
'''
Admin panel functionalities.
'''
from models import User, Provider, ServiceRequest, connect_db
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox

def admin_panel():
    admin_root = tk.Tk()
    admin_root.title("Admin Panel")

    def list_users():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('SELECT * FROM users')
        users = cursor.fetchall()
        conn.close()
        messagebox.showinfo("Users", "\n".join([f"ID: {u[0]}, Username: {u[1]}" for u in users]))

    def list_providers():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('SELECT * FROM providers')
        providers = cursor.fetchall()
        conn.close()
        messagebox.showinfo("Providers", "\n".join([f"ID: {p[0]}, Name: {p[1]}, Service: {p[2]}" for p in providers]))

    def list_service_requests():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('SELECT * FROM service_requests')
        requests = cursor.fetchall()
        conn.close()
        messagebox.showinfo("Service Requests", "\n".join([f"ID: {r[0]}, Customer ID: {r[1]}, Provider ID: {r[2]}, Details: {r[3]}" for r in requests]))

    tk.Button(admin_root, text='List Users', command=list_users).pack(pady=5)
    tk.Button(admin_root, text='List Providers', command=list_providers).pack(pady=5)
    tk.Button(admin_root, text='List Service Requests', command=list_service_requests).pack(pady=5)

    admin_root.mainloop()
```

These modifications include implementing basic functionalities for the admin panel, allowing the admin to list users, providers, and service requests. This setup can be further expanded to include adding, updating, and deleting entries as needed.

```python
        ''')

        conn.commit()

    def __init__(self, customer_id, provider_id, details):
        self.customer_id = customer_id
        self.provider_id = provider_id
        self.details = details

    def to_dict(self):
        return {'customer_id': self.customer_id, 'provider_id': self.provider_id, 'details': self.details}

    @staticmethod
    def create_table():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS service_requests (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                customer_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
                provider_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
                details TEXT NOT NULL,
                FOREIGN KEY (customer_id) REFERENCES users(id),
                FOREIGN KEY (provider_id) REFERENCES providers(id)
            )
        ''')
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()

    @staticmethod
    def add_request(customer_id, provider_id, details):
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('INSERT INTO service_requests (customer_id, provider_id, details) VALUES (?, ?, ?)', (customer_id, provider_id, details))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()

class Invoice:
    def __init__(self, service_request_id, amount):
        self.service_request_id = service_request_id
        self.amount = amount
        self.commission = amount * 0.05

    def to_dict(self):
        return {'service_request_id': self.service_request_id, 'amount': self.amount, 'commission': self.commission}

    @staticmethod
    def create_table():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS invoices (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                service_request_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
                amount REAL NOT NULL,
                commission REAL NOT NULL,
                FOREIGN KEY (service_request_id) REFERENCES service_requests(id)
            )
        ''')
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()

    @staticmethod
    def add_invoice(service_request_id, amount):
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        commission = amount * 0.05
        cursor.execute('INSERT INTO invoices (service_request_id, amount, commission) VALUES (?, ?, ?)', (service_request_id, amount, commission))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
```

auth.py
```python
'''
Handles user authentication.
'''
from models import User, connect_db

def authenticate_user(username, password):
    conn = connect_db()
    cursor = conn.cursor()
    cursor.execute('SELECT * FROM users WHERE username = ? AND password = ?', (username, password))
    user_data = cursor.fetchone()
    conn.close()
    if user_data:
        return User(user_data[1], user_data[2])
    return None
```

admin.py
```python
'''
Admin panel functionalities.
'''
from models import User, Provider, ServiceRequest, connect_db
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox

def admin_panel():
    admin_root = tk.Tk()
    admin_root.title("Admin Panel")

    def list_users():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('SELECT * FROM users')
        users = cursor.fetchall()
        conn.close()
        messagebox.showinfo("Users", "\n".join([f"ID: {u[0]}, Username: {u[1]}" for u in users]))

    def list_providers():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('SELECT * FROM providers')
        providers = cursor.fetchall()
        conn.close()
        messagebox.showinfo("Providers", "\n".join([f"ID: {p[0]}, Name: {p[1]}, Service: {p[2]}" for p in providers]))

    def list_service_requests():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('SELECT * FROM service_requests')
        requests = cursor.fetchall()
        conn.close()
        messagebox.showinfo("Service Requests", "\n".join([f"ID: {r[0]}, Customer ID: {r[1]}, Provider ID: {r[2]}, Details: {r[3]}" for r in requests]))

    tk.Button(admin_root, text='List Users', command=list_users).pack(pady=5)
    tk.Button(admin_root, text='List Providers', command=list_providers).pack(pady=5)
    tk.Button(admin_root, text='List Service Requests', command=list_service_requests).pack(pady=5)

    admin_root.mainloop()
```

These modifications include implementing basic functionalities for the admin panel, allowing the admin to list users, providers, and service requests. This setup can be further expanded to include adding, updating, and deleting entries as needed.

```python
'''
GUI implementation using Tkinter for user interaction.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox
from auth import authenticate_user
from admin import admin_panel
def create_gui():
    root = tk.Tk()
    root.title("On-Demand Service Platform")
    def login():
        username = username_entry.get()
        password = password_entry.get()
        user = authenticate_user(username, password)
        if user:
            messagebox.showinfo("Login", f"Logged in as {username}")
            if username == "admin":  # Assuming 'admin' is the admin username
                admin_panel()
        else:
            messagebox.showerror("Login Failed", "Invalid username or password")
    tk.Label(root, text="Username").grid(row=0)
    tk.Label(root, text="Password").grid(row=1)
    username_entry = tk.Entry(root)
    password_entry = tk.Entry(root, show='*')
    username_entry.grid(row=0, column=1)
    password_entry.grid(row=1, column=1)
    tk.Button(root, text='Login', command=login).grid(row=2, column=1, pady=4)
    root.mainloop()
if __name__ == '__main__':
    create_gui()
```

models.py
```python
'''
Contains classes for User, Provider, ServiceRequest, and Invoice to handle data and operations.
'''
import sqlite3
def connect_db():
    return sqlite3.connect('service_platform.db')
class User:
    def __init__(self, username, password):
        self.username = username
        self.password = password
    def to_dict(self):
        return {'username': self.username}
    @staticmethod
    def create_table():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS users (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                username TEXT NOT NULL UNIQUE,
                password TEXT NOT NULL
            )
        ''')
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
    @staticmethod
    def add_user(username, password):
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('INSERT INTO users (username, password) VALUES (?, ?)', (username, password))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
class Provider:
    def __init__(self, name, service_type):
        self.name = name
        self.service_type = service_type
    def to_dict(self):
        return {'name': self.name, 'service_type': self.service_type}
    @staticmethod
    def create_table():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS providers (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                name TEXT NOT NULL,
                service_type TEXT NOT NULL
            )
        ''')
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
    @staticmethod
    def add_provider(name, service_type):
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('INSERT INTO providers (name, service_type) VALUES (?, ?)', (name, service_type))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
class ServiceRequest:
    def __init__(self, customer_id, provider_id, details):
        self.customer_id = customer_id
        self.provider_id = provider_id
        self.details = details
    def to_dict(self):
        return {'customer_id': self.customer_id, 'provider_id': self.provider_id, 'details': self.details}
    @staticmethod
    def create_table():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS service_requests (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                customer_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
                provider_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
                details TEXT NOT NULL,
                FOREIGN KEY (customer_id) REFERENCES users(id),
                FOREIGN KEY (provider_id) REFERENCES providers(id)
            )
        ''')
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
    @staticmethod
    def add_request(customer_id, provider_id, details):
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('INSERT INTO service_requests (customer_id, provider_id, details) VALUES (?, ?, ?)', (customer_id, provider_id, details))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
class Invoice:
    def __init__(self, service_request_id, amount):
        self.service_request_id = service_request_id
        self.amount = amount
        self.commission = amount * 0.05
    def to_dict(self):
        return {'service_request_id': self.service_request_id, 'amount': self.amount, 'commission': self.commission}
    @staticmethod
    def create_table():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS invoices (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                service_request_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
                amount REAL NOT NULL,
                commission REAL NOT NULL,
                FOREIGN KEY (service_request_id) REFERENCES service_requests(id)
            )
        ''')
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
    @staticmethod
    def add_invoice(service_request_id, amount):
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        commission = amount * 0.05
        cursor.execute('INSERT INTO invoices (service_request_id, amount, commission) VALUES (?, ?, ?)', (service_request_id, amount, commission))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
```

auth.py
```python
'''
Handles user authentication.
'''
from models import User, connect_db
def authenticate_user(username, password):
    conn = connect_db()
    cursor = conn.cursor()
    cursor.execute('SELECT * FROM users WHERE username = ? AND password = ?', (username, password))
    user_data = cursor.fetchone()
    conn.close()
    if user_data:
        return User(user_data[1], user_data[2])
    return None
```

admin.py
```python
'''
Admin panel functionalities.
'''
from models import User, Provider, ServiceRequest, connect_db
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox
def admin_panel():
    admin_root = tk.Tk()
    admin_root.title("Admin Panel")
    def list_users():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('SELECT * FROM users')
        users = cursor.fetchall()
        conn.close()
        messagebox.showinfo("Users", "\n".join([f"ID: {u[0]}, Username: {u[1]}" for u in users]))
    def list_providers():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('SELECT * FROM providers')
        providers = cursor.fetchall()
        conn.close()
        messagebox.showinfo("Providers", "\n".join([f"ID: {p[0]}, Name: {p[1]}, Service: {p[2]}" for p in providers]))
    def list_service_requests():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('SELECT * FROM service_requests')
        requests = cursor.fetchall()
        conn.close()
        messagebox.showinfo("Service Requests", "\n".join([f"ID: {r[0]}, Customer ID: {r[1]}, Provider ID: {r[2]}, Details: {r[3]}" for r in requests]))
    tk.Button(admin_root, text='List Users', command=list_users).pack(pady=5)
    tk.Button(admin_root, text='List Providers', command=list_providers).pack(pady=5)
    tk.Button(admin_root, text='List Service Requests', command=list_service_requests).pack(pady=5)
    admin_root.mainloop()
```

The highest priority comment is regarding the security of user authentication. The current implementation stores passwords in plain text within the database, which poses a significant security risk. 

**Suggestion for Revision:**
1. Implement password hashing before storing passwords in the database. Use a library like `bcrypt` to hash passwords securely.
2. Update the `add_user` method in the `User` class to hash the password before inserting it into the database.
3. Modify the `authenticate_user` function to compare the hashed password stored in the database with the hash of the entered password.

Here is an example of how you can implement password hashing using `bcrypt`:

```python
import bcrypt

class User:
    # ... existing code ...

    @staticmethod
    def add_user(username, password):
        hashed_password = bcrypt.hashpw(password.encode('utf-8'), bcrypt.gensalt())
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('INSERT INTO users (username, password) VALUES (?, ?)', (username, hashed_password))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()

def authenticate_user(username, password):
    conn = connect_db()
    cursor = conn.cursor()
    cursor.execute('SELECT * FROM users WHERE username = ?', (username,))
    user_data = cursor.fetchone()
    conn.close()
    if user_data and bcrypt.checkpw(password.encode('utf-8'), user_data[2]):
        return User(user_data[1], user_data[2])
    return None
```

**Suggestion for Revision:**

```python
import bcrypt

    @staticmethod

        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('INSERT INTO users (username, password) VALUES (?, ?)', (username, hashed_password))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()

def authenticate_user(username, password):
    conn = connect_db()
    cursor = conn.cursor()
    cursor.execute('SELECT * FROM users WHERE username = ?', (username,))
    user_data = cursor.fetchone()
    conn.close()
    if user_data and bcrypt.checkpw(password.encode('utf-8'), user_data[2]):
        return User(user_data[1], user_data[2])
    return None
```

"main.py
```python
'''
GUI implementation using Tkinter for user interaction.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox
from auth import authenticate_user
from admin import admin_panel
def create_gui():
    root = tk.Tk()
    root.title("On-Demand Service Platform")
    def login():
        username = username_entry.get()
        password = password_entry.get()
        user = authenticate_user(username, password)
        if user:
            messagebox.showinfo("Login", f"Logged in as {username}")
            if username == "admin":  # Assuming 'admin' is the admin username
                admin_panel()
        else:
            messagebox.showerror("Login Failed", "Invalid username or password")
    tk.Label(root, text="Username").grid(row=0)
    tk.Label(root, text="Password").grid(row=1)
    username_entry = tk.Entry(root)
    password_entry = tk.Entry(root, show='*')
    username_entry.grid(row=0, column=1)
    password_entry.grid(row=1, column=1)
    tk.Button(root, text='Login', command=login).grid(row=2, column=1, pady=4)
    root.mainloop()
if __name__ == '__main__':
    create_gui()
```

models.py
```python
'''
Contains classes for User, Provider, ServiceRequest, and Invoice to handle data and operations.
'''
import sqlite3
def connect_db():
    return sqlite3.connect('service_platform.db')
class User:
    def __init__(self, username, password):
        self.username = username
        self.password = password
    def to_dict(self):
        return {'username': self.username}
    @staticmethod
    def create_table():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS users (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                username TEXT NOT NULL UNIQUE,
                password TEXT NOT NULL
            )
        ''')
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
    @staticmethod
    def add_user(username, password):
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('INSERT INTO users (username, password) VALUES (?, ?)', (username, password))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
class Provider:
    def __init__(self, name, service_type):
        self.name = name
        self.service_type = service_type
    def to_dict(self):
        return {'name': self.name, 'service_type': self.service_type}
    @staticmethod
    def create_table():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS providers (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                name TEXT NOT NULL,
                service_type TEXT NOT NULL
            )
        ''')
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
    @staticmethod
    def add_provider(name, service_type):
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('INSERT INTO providers (name, service_type) VALUES (?, ?)', (name, service_type))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
class ServiceRequest:
    def __init__(self, customer_id, provider_id, details):
        self.customer_id = customer_id
        self.provider_id = provider_id
        self.details = details
    def to_dict(self):
        return {'customer_id': self.customer_id, 'provider_id': self.provider_id, 'details': self.details}
    @staticmethod
    def create_table():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS service_requests (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                customer_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
                provider_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
                details TEXT NOT NULL,
                FOREIGN KEY (customer_id) REFERENCES users(id),
                FOREIGN KEY (provider_id) REFERENCES providers(id)
            )
        ''')
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
    @staticmethod
    def add_request(customer_id, provider_id, details):
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('INSERT INTO service_requests (customer_id, provider_id, details) VALUES (?, ?, ?)', (customer_id, provider_id, details))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
class Invoice:
    def __init__(self, service_request_id, amount):
        self.service_request_id = service_request_id
        self.amount = amount
        self.commission = amount * 0.05
    def to_dict(self):
        return {'service_request_id': self.service_request_id, 'amount': self.amount, 'commission': self.commission}
    @staticmethod
    def create_table():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS invoices (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                service_request_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
                amount REAL NOT NULL,
                commission REAL NOT NULL,
                FOREIGN KEY (service_request_id) REFERENCES service_requests(id)
            )
        ''')
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
    @staticmethod
    def add_invoice(service_request_id, amount):
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        commission = amount * 0.05
        cursor.execute('INSERT INTO invoices (service_request_id, amount, commission) VALUES (?, ?, ?)', (service_request_id, amount, commission))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
```

auth.py
```python
'''
Handles user authentication.
'''
from models import User, connect_db
def authenticate_user(username, password):
    conn = connect_db()
    cursor = conn.cursor()
    cursor.execute('SELECT * FROM users WHERE username = ? AND password = ?', (username, password))
    user_data = cursor.fetchone()
    conn.close()
    if user_data:
        return User(user_data[1], user_data[2])
    return None
```

admin.py
```python
'''
Admin panel functionalities.
'''
from models import User, Provider, ServiceRequest, connect_db
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox
def admin_panel():
    admin_root = tk.Tk()
    admin_root.title("Admin Panel")
    def list_users():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('SELECT * FROM users')
        users = cursor.fetchall()
        conn.close()
        messagebox.showinfo("Users", "\n".join([f"ID: {u[0]}, Username: {u[1]}" for u in users]))
    def list_providers():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('SELECT * FROM providers')
        providers = cursor.fetchall()
        conn.close()
        messagebox.showinfo("Providers", "\n".join([f"ID: {p[0]}, Name: {p[1]}, Service: {p[2]}" for p in providers]))
    def list_service_requests():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('SELECT * FROM service_requests')
        requests = cursor.fetchall()
        conn.close()
        messagebox.showinfo("Service Requests", "\n".join([f"ID: {r[0]}, Customer ID: {r[1]}, Provider ID: {r[2]}, Details: {r[3]}" for r in requests]))
    tk.Button(admin_root, text='List Users', command=list_users).pack(pady=5)
    tk.Button(admin_root, text='List Providers', command=list_providers).pack(pady=5)
    tk.Button(admin_root, text='List Service Requests', command=list_service_requests).pack(pady=5)
    admin_root.mainloop()
```

Comments on Codes:
"The highest priority comment is regarding the security of user authentication. The current implementation stores passwords in plain text within the database, which poses a significant security risk. 

**Suggestion for Revision:**
1. Implement password hashing before storing passwords in the database. Use a library like `bcrypt` to hash passwords securely.
2. Update the `add_user` method in the `User` class to hash the password before inserting it into the database.
3. Modify the `authenticate_user` function to compare the hashed password stored in the database with the hash of the entered password.

Here is an example of how you can implement password hashing using `bcrypt`:

```python
import bcrypt

class User:
    # ... existing code ...

    @staticmethod
    def add_user(username, password):
        hashed_password = bcrypt.hashpw(password.encode('utf-8'), bcrypt.gensalt())
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('INSERT INTO users (username, password) VALUES (?, ?)', (username, hashed_password))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()

def authenticate_user(username, password):
    conn = connect_db()
    cursor = conn.cursor()
    cursor.execute('SELECT * FROM users WHERE username = ?', (username,))
    user_data = cursor.fetchone()
    conn.close()
    if user_data and bcrypt.checkpw(password.encode('utf-8'), user_data[2]):
        return User(user_data[1], user_data[2])
    return None
```

Implement these changes to enhance the security of the application."

```python
'''
GUI implementation using Tkinter for user interaction.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox
from auth import authenticate_user
from admin import admin_panel

def create_gui():
    root = tk.Tk()
    root.title("On-Demand Service Platform")

    def login():
        username = username_entry.get()
        password = password_entry.get()
        user = authenticate_user(username, password)
        if user:
            messagebox.showinfo("Login", f"Logged in as {username}")
            if username == "admin":  # Assuming 'admin' is the admin username
                admin_panel()
        else:
            messagebox.showerror("Login Failed", "Invalid username or password")

    tk.Label(root, text="Username").grid(row=0)
    tk.Label(root, text="Password").grid(row=1)
    username_entry = tk.Entry(root)
    password_entry = tk.Entry(root, show='*')
    username_entry.grid(row=0, column=1)
    password_entry.grid(row=1, column=1)
    tk.Button(root, text='Login', command=login).grid(row=2, column=1, pady=4)
    root.mainloop()

if __name__ == '__main__':
    create_gui()
```

```python
'''
Contains classes for User, Provider, ServiceRequest, and Invoice to handle data and operations.
'''
import sqlite3
import bcrypt

def connect_db():
    return sqlite3.connect('service_platform.db')

class User:
    def __init__(self, username, password):
        self.username = username
        self.password = password

    def to_dict(self):
        return {'username': self.username}

    @staticmethod
    def create_table():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS users (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                username TEXT NOT NULL UNIQUE,
                password TEXT NOT NULL
            )
        ''')
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()

    @staticmethod
    def add_user(username, password):
        hashed_password = bcrypt.hashpw(password.encode('utf-8'), bcrypt.gensalt())
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('INSERT INTO users (username, password) VALUES (?, ?)', (username, hashed_password))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()

class Provider:
    def __init__(self, name, service_type):
        self.name = name
        self.service_type = service_type

    def to_dict(self):
        return {'name': self.name, 'service_type': self.service_type}

    @staticmethod
    def create_table():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS providers (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                name TEXT NOT NULL,
                service_type TEXT NOT NULL
            )
        ''')
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()

    @staticmethod
    def add_provider(name, service_type):
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('INSERT INTO providers (name, service_type) VALUES (?, ?)', (name, service_type))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()

class ServiceRequest:
    def __init__(self, customer_id, provider_id, details):
        self.customer_id = customer_id
        self.provider_id = provider_id
        self.details = details

    def to_dict(self):
        return {'customer_id': self.customer_id, 'provider_id': self.provider_id, 'details': self.details}

    @staticmethod
    def create_table():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS service_requests (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                customer_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
                provider_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
                details TEXT NOT NULL,
                FOREIGN KEY (customer_id) REFERENCES users(id),
                FOREIGN KEY (provider_id) REFERENCES providers(id)
            )
        ''')
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()

    @staticmethod
    def add_request(customer_id, provider_id, details):
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('INSERT INTO service_requests (customer_id, provider_id, details) VALUES (?, ?, ?)', (customer_id, provider_id, details))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()

class Invoice:
    def __init__(self, service_request_id, amount):
        self.service_request_id = service_request_id
        self.amount = amount
        self.commission = amount * 0.05

    def to_dict(self):
        return {'service_request_id': self.service_request_id, 'amount': self.amount, 'commission': self.commission}

    @staticmethod
    def create_table():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS invoices (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                service_request_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
                amount REAL NOT NULL,
                commission REAL NOT NULL,
                FOREIGN KEY (service_request_id) REFERENCES service_requests(id)
            )
        ''')
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()

    @staticmethod
    def add_invoice(service_request_id, amount):
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        commission = amount * 0.05
        cursor.execute('INSERT INTO invoices (service_request_id, amount, commission) VALUES (?, ?, ?)', (service_request_id, amount, commission))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
```

auth.py
```python
'''
Handles user authentication.
'''
from models import User, connect_db
import bcrypt

def authenticate_user(username, password):
    conn = connect_db()
    cursor = conn.cursor()
    cursor.execute('SELECT * FROM users WHERE username = ?', (username,))
    user_data = cursor.fetchone()
    conn.close()
    if user_data and bcrypt.checkpw(password.encode('utf-8'), user_data[2]):
        return User(user_data[1], user_data[2])
    return None
```

admin.py
```python
'''
Admin panel functionalities.
'''
from models import User, Provider, ServiceRequest, connect_db
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox

def admin_panel():
    admin_root = tk.Tk()
    admin_root.title("Admin Panel")

    def list_users():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('SELECT * FROM users')
        users = cursor.fetchall()
        conn.close()
        messagebox.showinfo("Users", "\n".join([f"ID: {u[0]}, Username: {u[1]}" for u in users]))

    def list_providers():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('SELECT * FROM providers')
        providers = cursor.fetchall()
        conn.close()
        messagebox.showinfo("Providers", "\n".join([f"ID: {p[0]}, Name: {p[1]}, Service: {p[2]}" for p in providers]))

    def list_service_requests():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('SELECT * FROM service_requests')
        requests = cursor.fetchall()
        conn.close()
        messagebox.showinfo("Service Requests", "\n".join([f"ID: {r[0]}, Customer ID: {r[1]}, Provider ID: {r[2]}, Details: {r[3]}" for r in requests]))

    tk.Button(admin_root, text='List Users', command=list_users).pack(pady=5)
    tk.Button(admin_root, text='List Providers', command=list_providers).pack(pady=5)
    tk.Button(admin_root, text='List Service Requests', command=list_service_requests).pack(pady=5)
    admin_root.mainloop()
```

**[Seminar Conclusion]**:

 main.py
```python
'''
GUI implementation using Tkinter for user interaction.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox
from auth import authenticate_user
from admin import admin_panel

def create_gui():
    root = tk.Tk()
    root.title("On-Demand Service Platform")

    def login():
        username = username_entry.get()
        password = password_entry.get()
        user = authenticate_user(username, password)
        if user:
            messagebox.showinfo("Login", f"Logged in as {username}")
            if username == "admin":  # Assuming 'admin' is the admin username
                admin_panel()
        else:
            messagebox.showerror("Login Failed", "Invalid username or password")

    tk.Label(root, text="Username").grid(row=0)
    tk.Label(root, text="Password").grid(row=1)
    username_entry = tk.Entry(root)
    password_entry = tk.Entry(root, show='*')
    username_entry.grid(row=0, column=1)
    password_entry.grid(row=1, column=1)
    tk.Button(root, text='Login', command=login).grid(row=2, column=1, pady=4)
    root.mainloop()

if __name__ == '__main__':
    create_gui()
```

models.py
```python
'''
Contains classes for User, Provider, ServiceRequest, and Invoice to handle data and operations.
'''
import sqlite3
import bcrypt

def connect_db():
    return sqlite3.connect('service_platform.db')

class User:
    def __init__(self, username, password):
        self.username = username
        self.password = password

    def to_dict(self):
        return {'username': self.username}

    @staticmethod
    def create_table():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS users (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                username TEXT NOT NULL UNIQUE,
                password TEXT NOT NULL
            )
        ''')
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()

    @staticmethod
    def add_user(username, password):
        hashed_password = bcrypt.hashpw(password.encode('utf-8'), bcrypt.gensalt())
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('INSERT INTO users (username, password) VALUES (?, ?)', (username, hashed_password))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()

class Provider:
    def __init__(self, name, service_type):
        self.name = name
        self.service_type = service_type

    def to_dict(self):
        return {'name': self.name, 'service_type': self.service_type}

    @staticmethod
    def create_table():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS providers (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                name TEXT NOT NULL,
                service_type TEXT NOT NULL
            )
        ''')
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()

    @staticmethod
    def add_provider(name, service_type):
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('INSERT INTO providers (name, service_type) VALUES (?, ?)', (name, service_type))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()

class ServiceRequest:
    def __init__(self, customer_id, provider_id, details):
        self.customer_id = customer_id
        self.provider_id = provider_id
        self.details = details

    def to_dict(self):
        return {'customer_id': self.customer_id, 'provider_id': self.provider_id, 'details': self.details}

    @staticmethod
    def create_table():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS service_requests (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                customer_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
                provider_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
                details TEXT NOT NULL,
                FOREIGN KEY (customer_id) REFERENCES users(id),
                FOREIGN KEY (provider_id) REFERENCES providers(id)
            )
        ''')
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()

    @staticmethod
    def add_request(customer_id, provider_id, details):
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('INSERT INTO service_requests (customer_id, provider_id, details) VALUES (?, ?, ?)', (customer_id, provider_id, details))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()

class Invoice:
    def __init__(self, service_request_id, amount):
        self.service_request_id = service_request_id
        self.amount = amount
        self.commission = amount * 0.05

    def to_dict(self):
        return {'service_request_id': self.service_request_id, 'amount': self.amount, 'commission': self.commission}

    @staticmethod
    def create_table():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS invoices (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                service_request_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
                amount REAL NOT NULL,
                commission REAL NOT NULL,
                FOREIGN KEY (service_request_id) REFERENCES service_requests(id)
            )
        ''')
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()

    @staticmethod
    def add_invoice(service_request_id, amount):
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        commission = amount * 0.05
        cursor.execute('INSERT INTO invoices (service_request_id, amount, commission) VALUES (?, ?, ?)', (service_request_id, amount, commission))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
```

auth.py
```python
'''
Handles user authentication.
'''
from models import User, connect_db
import bcrypt

def authenticate_user(username, password):
    conn = connect_db()
    cursor = conn.cursor()
    cursor.execute('SELECT * FROM users WHERE username = ?', (username,))
    user_data = cursor.fetchone()
    conn.close()
    if user_data and bcrypt.checkpw(password.encode('utf-8'), user_data[2]):
        return User(user_data[1], user_data[2])
    return None
```
