"main.py
```python
'''
GUI implementation using Tkinter for user interaction.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox
from auth import authenticate_user
from admin import admin_panel
def create_gui():
    root = tk.Tk()
    root.title("On-Demand Service Platform")
    def login():
        username = username_entry.get()
        password = password_entry.get()
        user = authenticate_user(username, password)
        if user:
            messagebox.showinfo("Login", f"Logged in as {username}")
            if username == "admin":  # Assuming 'admin' is the admin username
                admin_panel()
        else:
            messagebox.showerror("Login Failed", "Invalid username or password")
    tk.Label(root, text="Username").grid(row=0)
    tk.Label(root, text="Password").grid(row=1)
    username_entry = tk.Entry(root)
    password_entry = tk.Entry(root, show='*')
    username_entry.grid(row=0, column=1)
    password_entry.grid(row=1, column=1)
    tk.Button(root, text='Login', command=login).grid(row=2, column=1, pady=4)
    root.mainloop()
if __name__ == '__main__':
    create_gui()
```

models.py
```python
'''
Contains classes for User, Provider, ServiceRequest, and Invoice to handle data and operations.
'''
import sqlite3
import bcrypt
def connect_db():
    return sqlite3.connect('service_platform.db')
class User:
    def __init__(self, username, password):
        self.username = username
        self.password = password
    def to_dict(self):
        return {'username': self.username}
    @staticmethod
    def create_table():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS users (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                username TEXT NOT NULL UNIQUE,
                password TEXT NOT NULL
            )
        ''')
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
    @staticmethod
    def add_user(username, password):
        hashed_password = bcrypt.hashpw(password.encode('utf-8'), bcrypt.gensalt())
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('INSERT INTO users (username, password) VALUES (?, ?)', (username, hashed_password))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
class Provider:
    def __init__(self, name, service_type):
        self.name = name
        self.service_type = service_type
    def to_dict(self):
        return {'name': self.name, 'service_type': self.service_type}
    @staticmethod
    def create_table():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS providers (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                name TEXT NOT NULL,
                service_type TEXT NOT NULL
            )
        ''')
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
    @staticmethod
    def add_provider(name, service_type):
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('INSERT INTO providers (name, service_type) VALUES (?, ?)', (name, service_type))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
class ServiceRequest:
    def __init__(self, customer_id, provider_id, details):
        self.customer_id = customer_id
        self.provider_id = provider_id
        self.details = details
    def to_dict(self):
        return {'customer_id': self.customer_id, 'provider_id': self.provider_id, 'details': self.details}
    @staticmethod
    def create_table():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS service_requests (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                customer_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
                provider_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
                details TEXT NOT NULL,
                FOREIGN KEY (customer_id) REFERENCES users(id),
                FOREIGN KEY (provider_id) REFERENCES providers(id)
            )
        ''')
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
    @staticmethod
    def add_request(customer_id, provider_id, details):
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('INSERT INTO service_requests (customer_id, provider_id, details) VALUES (?, ?, ?)', (customer_id, provider_id, details))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
class Invoice:
    def __init__(self, service_request_id, amount):
        self.service_request_id = service_request_id
        self.amount = amount
        self.commission = amount * 0.05
    def to_dict(self):
        return {'service_request_id': self.service_request_id, 'amount': self.amount, 'commission': self.commission}
    @staticmethod
    def create_table():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS invoices (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                service_request_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
                amount REAL NOT NULL,
                commission REAL NOT NULL,
                FOREIGN KEY (service_request_id) REFERENCES service_requests(id)
            )
        ''')
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
    @staticmethod
    def add_invoice(service_request_id, amount):
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        commission = amount * 0.05
        cursor.execute('INSERT INTO invoices (service_request_id, amount, commission) VALUES (?, ?, ?)', (service_request_id, amount, commission))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
```

auth.py
```python
'''
Handles user authentication.
'''
from models import User, connect_db
import bcrypt
def authenticate_user(username, password):
    conn = connect_db()
    cursor = conn.cursor()
    cursor.execute('SELECT * FROM users WHERE username = ?', (username,))
    user_data = cursor.fetchone()
    conn.close()
    if user_data and bcrypt.checkpw(password.encode('utf-8'), user_data[2]):
        return User(user_data[1], user_data[2])
    return None
```

admin.py
```python
'''
Admin panel functionalities.
'''
from models import User, Provider, ServiceRequest, connect_db
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox
def admin_panel():
    admin_root = tk.Tk()
    admin_root.title("Admin Panel")
    def list_users():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('SELECT * FROM users')
        users = cursor.fetchall()
        conn.close()
        messagebox.showinfo("Users", "\n".join([f"ID: {u[0]}, Username: {u[1]}" for u in users]))
    def list_providers():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('SELECT * FROM providers')
        providers = cursor.fetchall()
        conn.close()
        messagebox.showinfo("Providers", "\n".join([f"ID: {p[0]}, Name: {p[1]}, Service: {p[2]}" for p in providers]))
    def list_service_requests():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('SELECT * FROM service_requests')
        requests = cursor.fetchall()
        conn.close()
        messagebox.showinfo("Service Requests", "\n".join([f"ID: {r[0]}, Customer ID: {r[1]}, Provider ID: {r[2]}, Details: {r[3]}" for r in requests]))
    tk.Button(admin_root, text='List Users', command=list_users).pack(pady=5)
    tk.Button(admin_root, text='List Providers', command=list_providers).pack(pady=5)
    tk.Button(admin_root, text='List Service Requests', command=list_service_requests).pack(pady=5)
    admin_root.mainloop()
```

"main.py
```python
'''
GUI implementation using Tkinter for user interaction.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox
from auth import authenticate_user
from admin import admin_panel
def create_gui():
    root = tk.Tk()
    root.title("On-Demand Service Platform")
    def login():
        username = username_entry.get()
        password = password_entry.get()
        user = authenticate_user(username, password)
        if user:
            messagebox.showinfo("Login", f"Logged in as {username}")
            if username == "admin":  # Assuming 'admin' is the admin username
                admin_panel()
        else:
            messagebox.showerror("Login Failed", "Invalid username or password")
    tk.Label(root, text="Username").grid(row=0)
    tk.Label(root, text="Password").grid(row=1)
    username_entry = tk.Entry(root)
    password_entry = tk.Entry(root, show='*')
    username_entry.grid(row=0, column=1)
    password_entry.grid(row=1, column=1)
    tk.Button(root, text='Login', command=login).grid(row=2, column=1, pady=4)
    root.mainloop()
if __name__ == '__main__':
    create_gui()
```

models.py
```python
'''
Contains classes for User, Provider, ServiceRequest, and Invoice to handle data and operations.
'''
import sqlite3
import bcrypt
def connect_db():
    return sqlite3.connect('service_platform.db')
class User:
    def __init__(self, username, password):
        self.username = username
        self.password = password
    def to_dict(self):
        return {'username': self.username}
    @staticmethod
    def create_table():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS users (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                username TEXT NOT NULL UNIQUE,
                password TEXT NOT NULL
            )
        ''')
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
    @staticmethod
    def add_user(username, password):
        hashed_password = bcrypt.hashpw(password.encode('utf-8'), bcrypt.gensalt())
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('INSERT INTO users (username, password) VALUES (?, ?)', (username, hashed_password))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
class Provider:
    def __init__(self, name, service_type):
        self.name = name
        self.service_type = service_type
    def to_dict(self):
        return {'name': self.name, 'service_type': self.service_type}
    @staticmethod
    def create_table():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS providers (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                name TEXT NOT NULL,
                service_type TEXT NOT NULL
            )
        ''')
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
    @staticmethod
    def add_provider(name, service_type):
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('INSERT INTO providers (name, service_type) VALUES (?, ?)', (name, service_type))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
class ServiceRequest:
    def __init__(self, customer_id, provider_id, details):
        self.customer_id = customer_id
        self.provider_id = provider_id
        self.details = details
    def to_dict(self):
        return {'customer_id': self.customer_id, 'provider_id': self.provider_id, 'details': self.details}
    @staticmethod
    def create_table():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS service_requests (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                customer_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
                provider_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
                details TEXT NOT NULL,
                FOREIGN KEY (customer_id) REFERENCES users(id),
                FOREIGN KEY (provider_id) REFERENCES providers(id)
            )
        ''')
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
    @staticmethod
    def add_request(customer_id, provider_id, details):
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('INSERT INTO service_requests (customer_id, provider_id, details) VALUES (?, ?, ?)', (customer_id, provider_id, details))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
class Invoice:
    def __init__(self, service_request_id, amount):
        self.service_request_id = service_request_id
        self.amount = amount
        self.commission = amount * 0.05
    def to_dict(self):
        return {'service_request_id': self.service_request_id, 'amount': self.amount, 'commission': self.commission}
    @staticmethod
    def create_table():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS invoices (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                service_request_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
                amount REAL NOT NULL,
                commission REAL NOT NULL,
                FOREIGN KEY (service_request_id) REFERENCES service_requests(id)
            )
        ''')
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
    @staticmethod
    def add_invoice(service_request_id, amount):
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        commission = amount * 0.05
        cursor.execute('INSERT INTO invoices (service_request_id, amount, commission) VALUES (?, ?, ?)', (service_request_id, amount, commission))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
```

auth.py
```python
'''
Handles user authentication.
'''
from models import User, connect_db
import bcrypt
def authenticate_user(username, password):
    conn = connect_db()
    cursor = conn.cursor()
    cursor.execute('SELECT * FROM users WHERE username = ?', (username,))
    user_data = cursor.fetchone()
    conn.close()
    if user_data and bcrypt.checkpw(password.encode('utf-8'), user_data[2]):
        return User(user_data[1], user_data[2])
    return None
```

admin.py
```python
'''
Admin panel functionalities.
'''
from models import User, Provider, ServiceRequest, connect_db
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox
def admin_panel():
    admin_root = tk.Tk()
    admin_root.title("Admin Panel")
    def list_users():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('SELECT * FROM users')
        users = cursor.fetchall()
        conn.close()
        messagebox.showinfo("Users", "\n".join([f"ID: {u[0]}, Username: {u[1]}" for u in users]))
    def list_providers():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('SELECT * FROM providers')
        providers = cursor.fetchall()
        conn.close()
        messagebox.showinfo("Providers", "\n".join([f"ID: {p[0]}, Name: {p[1]}, Service: {p[2]}" for p in providers]))
    def list_service_requests():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('SELECT * FROM service_requests')
        requests = cursor.fetchall()
        conn.close()
        messagebox.showinfo("Service Requests", "\n".join([f"ID: {r[0]}, Customer ID: {r[1]}, Provider ID: {r[2]}, Details: {r[3]}" for r in requests]))
    tk.Button(admin_root, text='List Users', command=list_users).pack(pady=5)
    tk.Button(admin_root, text='List Providers', command=list_providers).pack(pady=5)
    tk.Button(admin_root, text='List Service Requests', command=list_service_requests).pack(pady=5)
    admin_root.mainloop()
```

"main.py
```python
'''
GUI implementation using Tkinter for user interaction.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox
from auth import authenticate_user
from admin import admin_panel
def create_gui():
    root = tk.Tk()
    root.title("On-Demand Service Platform")
    def login():
        username = username_entry.get()
        password = password_entry.get()
        user = authenticate_user(username, password)
        if user:
            messagebox.showinfo("Login", f"Logged in as {username}")
            if username == "admin":  # Assuming 'admin' is the admin username
                admin_panel()
        else:
            messagebox.showerror("Login Failed", "Invalid username or password")
    tk.Label(root, text="Username").grid(row=0)
    tk.Label(root, text="Password").grid(row=1)
    username_entry = tk.Entry(root)
    password_entry = tk.Entry(root, show='*')
    username_entry.grid(row=0, column=1)
    password_entry.grid(row=1, column=1)
    tk.Button(root, text='Login', command=login).grid(row=2, column=1, pady=4)
    root.mainloop()
if __name__ == '__main__':
    create_gui()
```

models.py
```python
'''
Contains classes for User, Provider, ServiceRequest, and Invoice to handle data and operations.
'''
import sqlite3
import bcrypt
def connect_db():
    return sqlite3.connect('service_platform.db')
class User:
    def __init__(self, username, password):
        self.username = username
        self.password = password
    def to_dict(self):
        return {'username': self.username}
    @staticmethod
    def create_table():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS users (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                username TEXT NOT NULL UNIQUE,
                password TEXT NOT NULL
            )
        ''')
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
    @staticmethod
    def add_user(username, password):
        hashed_password = bcrypt.hashpw(password.encode('utf-8'), bcrypt.gensalt())
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('INSERT INTO users (username, password) VALUES (?, ?)', (username, hashed_password))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
class Provider:
    def __init__(self, name, service_type):
        self.name = name
        self.service_type = service_type
    def to_dict(self):
        return {'name': self.name, 'service_type': self.service_type}
    @staticmethod
    def create_table():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS providers (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                name TEXT NOT NULL,
                service_type TEXT NOT NULL
            )
        ''')
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
    @staticmethod
    def add_provider(name, service_type):
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('INSERT INTO providers (name, service_type) VALUES (?, ?)', (name, service_type))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
class ServiceRequest:
    def __init__(self, customer_id, provider_id, details):
        self.customer_id = customer_id
        self.provider_id = provider_id
        self.details = details
    def to_dict(self):
        return {'customer_id': self.customer_id, 'provider_id': self.provider_id, 'details': self.details}
    @staticmethod
    def create_table():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS service_requests (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                customer_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
                provider_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
                details TEXT NOT NULL,
                FOREIGN KEY (customer_id) REFERENCES users(id),
                FOREIGN KEY (provider_id) REFERENCES providers(id)
            )
        ''')
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
    @staticmethod
    def add_request(customer_id, provider_id, details):
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('INSERT INTO service_requests (customer_id, provider_id, details) VALUES (?, ?, ?)', (customer_id, provider_id, details))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
class Invoice:
    def __init__(self, service_request_id, amount):
        self.service_request_id = service_request_id
        self.amount = amount
        self.commission = amount * 0.05
    def to_dict(self):
        return {'service_request_id': self.service_request_id, 'amount': self.amount, 'commission': self.commission}
    @staticmethod
    def create_table():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS invoices (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                service_request_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
                amount REAL NOT NULL,
                commission REAL NOT NULL,
                FOREIGN KEY (service_request_id) REFERENCES service_requests(id)
            )
        ''')
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
    @staticmethod
    def add_invoice(service_request_id, amount):
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        commission = amount * 0.05
        cursor.execute('INSERT INTO invoices (service_request_id, amount, commission) VALUES (?, ?, ?)', (service_request_id, amount, commission))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
```
auth.py
```python
'''
Handles user authentication.
'''
from models import User, connect_db
import bcrypt
def authenticate_user(username, password):
    conn = connect_db()
    cursor = conn.cursor()
    cursor.execute('SELECT * FROM users WHERE username = ?', (username,))
    user_data = cursor.fetchone()
    conn.close()
    if user_data and bcrypt.checkpw(password.encode('utf-8'), user_data[2]):
        return User(user_data[1], user_data[2])
    return None
```
admin.py
```python
'''
Admin panel functionalities.
'''
from models import User, Provider, ServiceRequest, connect_db
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox
def admin_panel():
    admin_root = tk.Tk()
    admin_root.title("Admin Panel")
    def list_users():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('SELECT * FROM users')
        users = cursor.fetchall()
        conn.close()
        messagebox.showinfo("Users", "\n".join([f"ID: {u[0]}, Username: {u[1]}" for u in users]))
    def list_providers():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('SELECT * FROM providers')
        providers = cursor.fetchall()
        conn.close()
        messagebox.showinfo("Providers", "\n".join([f"ID: {p[0]}, Name: {p[1]}, Service: {p[2]}" for p in providers]))
    def list_service_requests():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('SELECT * FROM service_requests')
        requests = cursor.fetchall()
        conn.close()
        messagebox.showinfo("Service Requests", "\n".join([f"ID: {r[0]}, Customer ID: {r[1]}, Provider ID: {r[2]}, Details: {r[3]}" for r in requests]))
    tk.Button(admin_root, text='List Users', command=list_users).pack(pady=5)
    tk.Button(admin_root, text='List Providers', command=list_providers).pack(pady=5)
    tk.Button(admin_root, text='List Service Requests', command=list_service_requests).pack(pady=5)
    admin_root.mainloop()
```

```python
'''
GUI implementation using Tkinter for user interaction.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox
from auth import authenticate_user
from admin import admin_panel
def create_gui():
    root = tk.Tk()
    root.title("On-Demand Service Platform")
    def login():
        username = username_entry.get()
        password = password_entry.get()
        user = authenticate_user(username, password)
        if user:
            messagebox.showinfo("Login", f"Logged in as {username}")
            if username == "admin":  # Assuming 'admin' is the admin username
                admin_panel()
        else:
            messagebox.showerror("Login Failed", "Invalid username or password")
    tk.Label(root, text="Username").grid(row=0)
    tk.Label(root, text="Password").grid(row=1)
    username_entry = tk.Entry(root)
    password_entry = tk.Entry(root, show='*')
    username_entry.grid(row=0, column=1)
    password_entry.grid(row=1, column=1)
    tk.Button(root, text='Login', command=login).grid(row=2, column=1, pady=4)
    root.mainloop()
if __name__ == '__main__':
    create_gui()
```

models.py
```python
'''
Contains classes for User, Provider, ServiceRequest, and Invoice to handle data and operations.
'''
import sqlite3
import bcrypt
def connect_db():
    return sqlite3.connect('service_platform.db')
class User:
    def __init__(self, username, password):
        self.username = username
        self.password = password
    def to_dict(self):
        return {'username': self.username}
    @staticmethod
    def create_table():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS users (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                username TEXT NOT NULL UNIQUE,
                password TEXT NOT NULL
            )
        ''')
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
    @staticmethod
    def add_user(username, password):
        hashed_password = bcrypt.hashpw(password.encode('utf-8'), bcrypt.gensalt())
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('INSERT INTO users (username, password) VALUES (?, ?)', (username, hashed_password))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
class Provider:
    def __init__(self, name, service_type):
        self.name = name
        self.service_type = service_type
    def to_dict(self):
        return {'name': self.name, 'service_type': self.service_type}
    @staticmethod
    def create_table():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS providers (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                name TEXT NOT NULL,
                service_type TEXT NOT NULL
            )
        ''')
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
    @staticmethod
    def add_provider(name, service_type):
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('INSERT INTO providers (name, service_type) VALUES (?, ?)', (name, service_type))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
class ServiceRequest:
    def __init__(self, customer_id, provider_id, details):
        self.customer_id = customer_id
        self.provider_id = provider_id
        self.details = details
    def to_dict(self):
        return {'customer_id': self.customer_id, 'provider_id': self.provider_id, 'details': self.details}
    @staticmethod
    def create_table():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS service_requests (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                customer_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
                provider_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
                details TEXT NOT NULL,
                FOREIGN KEY (customer_id) REFERENCES users(id),
                FOREIGN KEY (provider_id) REFERENCES providers(id)
            )
        ''')
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
    @staticmethod
    def add_request(customer_id, provider_id, details):
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('INSERT INTO service_requests (customer_id, provider_id, details) VALUES (?, ?, ?)', (customer_id, provider_id, details))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
class Invoice:
    def __init__(self, service_request_id, amount):
        self.service_request_id = service_request_id
        self.amount = amount
        self.commission = amount * 0.05
    def to_dict(self):
        return {'service_request_id': self.service_request_id, 'amount': self.amount, 'commission': self.commission}
    @staticmethod
    def create_table():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS invoices (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                service_request_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
                amount REAL NOT NULL,
                commission REAL NOT NULL,
                FOREIGN KEY (service_request_id) REFERENCES service_requests(id)
            )
        ''')
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
    @staticmethod
    def add_invoice(service_request_id, amount):
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        commission = amount * 0.05
        cursor.execute('INSERT INTO invoices (service_request_id, amount, commission) VALUES (?, ?, ?)', (service_request_id, amount, commission))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
```

auth.py
```python
'''
Handles user authentication.
'''
from models import User, connect_db
import bcrypt
def authenticate_user(username, password):
    conn = connect_db()
    cursor = conn.cursor()
    cursor.execute('SELECT * FROM users WHERE username = ?', (username,))
    user_data = cursor.fetchone()
    conn.close()
    if user_data and bcrypt.checkpw(password.encode('utf-8'), user_data[2]):
        return User(user_data[1], user_data[2])
    return None
```

admin.py
```python
'''
Admin panel functionalities.
'''
from models import User, Provider, ServiceRequest, connect_db
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox
def admin_panel():
    admin_root = tk.Tk()
    admin_root.title("Admin Panel")
    def list_users():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('SELECT * FROM users')
        users = cursor.fetchall()
        conn.close()
        messagebox.showinfo("Users", "\n".join([f"ID: {u[0]}, Username: {u[1]}" for u in users]))
    def list_providers():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('SELECT * FROM providers')
        providers = cursor.fetchall()
        conn.close()
        messagebox.showinfo("Providers", "\n".join([f"ID: {p[0]}, Name: {p[1]}, Service: {p[2]}" for p in providers]))
    def list_service_requests():
        conn = connect_db()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('SELECT * FROM service_requests')
        requests = cursor.fetchall()
        conn.close()
        messagebox.showinfo("Service Requests", "\n".join([f"ID: {r[0]}, Customer ID: {r[1]}, Provider ID: {r[2]}, Details: {r[3]}" for r in requests]))
    tk.Button(admin_root, text='List Users', command=list_users).pack(pady=5)
    tk.Button(admin_root, text='List Providers', command=list_providers).pack(pady=5)
    tk.Button(admin_root, text='List Service Requests', command=list_service_requests).pack(pady=5)
    admin_root.mainloop()
```
```

Large language models (LLMs) are emerging as a transformative technology, enabling developers to build applications that they previously could not. # On-Demand Service Platform
```

This software is a Python-based application designed to connect customers with on-demand service providers. It includes features such as user authentication, provider profiles, service requests, live status updates, invoicing with a 5% commission, and an admin panel for management.

## Main Functions

### User Authentication
- Users can log in to the platform using their username and password.
- The system verifies credentials and grants access accordingly.

### Provider Profiles
- Service providers can create profiles detailing their services.
- Profiles include the provider's name and type of service offered.

### Service Requests
- Customers can request services from providers.
- Each request includes details about the service needed and links to both the customer and provider.

### Live Status Updates
- The platform can be extended to include real-time updates on service requests (not implemented in the current version).

### Invoicing
- Invoices are generated for each service request.
- A 5% commission is automatically calculated and included in the invoice.

### Admin Panel
- Admin users can access a panel to manage users, providers, and service requests.
- The panel allows listing all users, providers, and service requests.

## Installation

### Prerequisites
- Python 3.x
- SQLite (for database management)

### Quick Install

1. **Clone the Repository**
   ```bash
   git clone <repository-url>
   cd <repository-directory>
   ```

2. **Install Dependencies**
   Ensure you have `pip` installed, then run:
   ```bash
   pip install -r requirements.txt
   ```

3. **Set Up the Database**
   Run the following Python script to create necessary tables:
   ```bash
   python -c "from models import User, Provider, ServiceRequest, Invoice; User.create_table(); Provider.create_table(); ServiceRequest.create_table(); Invoice.create_table()"
   ```

## How to Use

1. **Run the Application**
   Execute the main script to start the GUI:
   ```bash
   python main.py
   ```

2. **Logging In**
   - Enter your username and password in the login window.
   - If you are an admin, you will have access to the admin panel.

3. **Admin Panel**
   - Accessible only to users with admin credentials.
   - Use the buttons to list users, providers, and service requests.

4. **Adding Users and Providers**
   - Currently, users and providers must be added directly to the database using the `add_user` and `add_provider` methods in `models.py`.

## Future Enhancements

- Implement live status updates for service requests.
- Develop a more comprehensive user interface for managing profiles and requests.
- Add functionality for users to register and manage their accounts directly through the GUI.

This manual provides a basic overview and instructions for using the On-Demand Service Platform. For any issues or further assistance, please contact our support team.
